{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2021-04-05 14:45:36","updatedTime":"2021-04-05 14:45:36","title":"This iPhone case gives your smartphone the Apple Mac Pro ‘cheesegrater’ texture","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=309067","description":"<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/the-cheesegrater-iphone-seemed-like-a-bad-idea-but-now-heres-what-it-would-actually-look-like/cheesegrater_iphone_1.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"702\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-309068\" /></p>\n<p>&#8220;Never knock an idea until you actually try it.&#8221;</p>\n<p>My opinion on the <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2019/06/03/the-latest-mac-pro-is-proof-that-apple-needs-to-step-up-its-design-game/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">2019 Mac Pro</a> has aged pretty well, I&#8217;d say. Sure, my reaction (which came just moments after the design was released) may have been premature, and so were the memes that followed the debut of the &#8216;cheesegrater Mac&#8217;&#8230; but even now, 2 years down the line, it feels slightly cathartic to know that my opinion hasn&#8217;t really changed &#8211; the 2019 Mac Pro still looks visibly odd and sort of gets my skin crawling.</p>\n<p>Recently though, the media discovered a patent for an iPhone that used the &#8216;cheesegrater&#8217; texture for efficient cooling or thermal transmission, and let&#8217;s just say, people weren&#8217;t happy. Some even legitimately debunked it as an April Fool&#8217;s Prank from Apple. My thoughts on the matter weren&#8217;t any different &#8211; it sounds like a terrible idea, but I thought the best thing to do would be to really give Apple the benefit of the doubt and MAKE a cheesegrater iPhone just so I have something to visually judge it by.</p>\n<p>Presenting, the &#8216;Cheesegrater&#8217; Case for the iPhone 12 Pro. Made from a TPE bumper and a machined aluminum backplate, the case puts the familiar cheesegrater texture on the back of the iPhone to help it cool more efficiently (well at least in theory). In theory, it&#8217;s also perfectly suited to mince cloves of garlic or grate some Parmigiano Reggiano.</p>\n<p>Now that we have a (sort of) clear vision of what the cheesegrater texture would look like on an iPhone, let&#8217;s objectively and subjectively judge this. For starters, it just looks like a really bad idea. Objectively speaking, a textured metal body would most certainly trap dirt, dust, pieces of lint, aside from also preventing the phone from wirelessly charging. The current textured metal plate is 1mm thick, and for any sort of texture, you&#8217;d need 3D depth which adds unnecessary thickness to the phone &#8211; something Apple probably won&#8217;t want to do. Subjectively speaking, the texture looks worse on the iPhone than on the Mac Pro (although it may also be my execution). Apple&#8217;s patent file states “the components of the electronic device may be designed to provide a unique and pleasing look and feel for a user”, a purpose that gets defeated when even Digital Trends calls it <a href=\"https://www.digitaltrends.com/computing/apple-patent-cheese-grater-design-iphone/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">&#8220;Apple&#8217;s worst-ever design idea&#8221;</a>. Moreover, at that scale, the texture could actually be used as a garlic press or a microplane for grating hard cheeses, which makes it difficult to take seriously when the texture is on a $1200 flagship smartphone. Let&#8217;s not even get into the &#8216;trypophobia&#8217; angle.</p>\n<p>My opinions aside, it seems like a weird idea for Apple to take such an extreme route for “enhanced levels of heat removal”. What exactly is the iPhone doing that it would even need desktop-grade heat removal? Is Apple going all-in on AR, or is it looking to put more powerful Apple-built silicone chips in their new iPhones? We&#8217;ll never really know. All we can say with a certain degree of confidence is that a &#8216;Cheesegrater&#8217; iPhone isn&#8217;t really a great idea&#8230;</p>\n<p>If you really want to make your own &#8216;Cheesegrater&#8217; iPhone case, you can download the 3D files by <a href=\"http://bit.ly/cheesegrateriphone\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">clicking here</a>.</p>\n<p>Designer/Visualizer: <a href=\"http://sarangsheth.net\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Sarang Sheth</a></p>\n<p><img publishedOrCreatedDate":1617605136671},{"createdTime":"2021-04-05 14:45:36","updatedTime":"2021-04-05 14:45:36","title":"Shenzhen’s new Institute of Design comes with a Hyper Roof & preserves the natural landscape","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=309000","description":"<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308996\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/308972/01_southernuniversityofscienceandtechnology_dominiqueperraultarchitecture_shenzheninstituteofdesignandinnovationcompetition.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>Shenzhen recently announced plans to build ‘ten new major cultural facilities’ over the span of three years and hosted international <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/category/architecture/\">architecture</a> <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/tag/competition/\">competitions</a> for structures like a <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2021/03/18/shenzhens-maritime-museum-is-a-hub-of-educational-experiences-that-resemble-a-cluster-of-glass-icebergs/\">future maritime museum</a>, music conservatory, opera house, and design institute. Since then, it’s been revealed that Dominique Perrault Architecture (DPA), in collaboration with Chinese design studio Zhubo Design Co., has won the international competition for the new campus of Shenzhen’s Institute of Design and Innovation.</p>\n<p>The new campus will form one of Southern University of Science and Technology’s future schools, located along the rural hillside of Shenzhen. Committed to preserving the natural landscape of Shenzhen’s rural region, the winning design embraces a large-scale horizontal campus that stretches for more than 700 meters. Comprised of two main areas that run parallel to one another, “Hyper-Ground” and “Hyper-Roof,” DPA planned the campus with sociability and sustainability in mind.</p>\n<p>The design’s “Hyper-Ground” component contains the chunk of the university’s services and meeting areas, including the library, auditorium, and exhibition halls. The design’s ground level consists of open-air social hubs woven throughout university infrastructure to promote hybridization of disciplines and design innovation. Chiseled throughout campus’ ground-level facilities in a pedestrian promenade where students and the public alike can enjoy various commercial services and access points to the university’s educational faculties.</p>\n<p>Filling out the winning design’s “Hyper-Roof,” students and the general public can escape from the social scene down below to garden spaces and outdoor sports areas. The “Hyper-Roof” also houses photovoltaic panels and a rainwater management system that provides the entire structure with energy. As the current layout acclimates to the preexisting landscape, its facade generally remains minimal in style, allowing room for even an amphitheater located near the campus’ main entrance.</p>\n<p>Designer: <a href=\"http://www.perraultarchitecture.com/en/homepage\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Dominique Perrault Architecture</a> x <a href=\"https://www.zhubo.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Zhubo Design Co.</a></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308995\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/308972/02_southernuniversityofscienceandtechnology_dominiqueperraultarchitecture_shenzheninstituteofdesignandinnovationcompetition.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>The new campus is located on the outskirts of Shenzhen&#8217;s rural region, below mountains and beside a nearby cityscape.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308994\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/auto-draft/03_southernuniversityofscienceandtechnology_dominiqueperraultarchitecture_shenzheninstituteofdesignandinnovationcompetition.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>The layout features a pedestrian promenade where students and the general public can meet and spend the day.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308993\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/auto-draft/04_southernuniversityofscienceandtechnology_dominiqueperraultarchitecture_shenzheninstituteofdesignandinnovationcompetition.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>The planned &#8220;Hyper-Roof&#8221; features garden spaces and sports areas, as well as photovoltaic panels and a rainwater management system.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308992\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/auto-draft/05_southernuniversityofscienceandtechnology_dominiqueperraultarchitecture_shenzheninstituteofdesignandinnovationcompetition.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>From the highway, the campus appears minimal and modest in design.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308991\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/auto-draft/06_southernuniversityofscienceandtechnology_dominiqueperraultarchitecture_shenzheninstituteofdesignandinnovationcompetition.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>Inside the campus, a blend of contemporary interior design and natural light create bright, open spaces.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308990\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/auto-draft/07_southernuniversityofscienceandtechnology_dominiqueperraultarchitecture_shenzheninstituteofdesignandinnovationcompetition.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308989\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/auto-draft/08_southernuniversityofscienceandtechnology_dominiqueperraultarchitecture_shenzheninstituteofdesignandinnovationcompetition.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>Comprised of two main structures, Dominique Perrault Architecture designed &#8220;Hyper-Ground&#8221; and &#8220;Hyper-Roof&#8221; levels.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308988\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/auto-draft/09_southernuniversityofscienceandtechnology_dominiqueperraultarchitecture_shenzheninstituteofdesignandinnovationcompetition.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>This section of the campus spans 700 meters in length.</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a width=\"1050\"></iframe></p>\n<p></span></p>\n<p></span></p>\n</div>\n<p>Run on the roads, jog on the beaches, trek mountain terrain, or even take a dip in the sea, Tropicfeel&#8217;s Jungle Shoes should serve you well through all of those endeavors. Designed to quite literally be the ATVs of footwear, the Jungle are a pair of shoes that prioritize two things &#8211; the journey, and comfort. They fit around your foot as comfortably as a sock would, and are equipped with a 3D Dual Cushion sole that lets you feel like you&#8217;re walking on air&#8230; even if you&#8217;re scaling mountains. The high-grip outsole gives you remarkable traction, while a special anti-abrasive 3D Mesh fabric made from plastic bottles protects your feet from the elements. With the use of unique materials, and even a few specially located drainage holes, the Jungle shoes can be worn underwater too. Whether you&#8217;re wading through a river or just swimming on the beach, the shoes form an extension of your foot, giving you freedom of movement. Take them off and they dry easily too&#8230; because they were designed to.</p>\n<p>If I had to entrust one company with creating the ultimate outdoor shoe, it would be Tropicfeel. A 26-person design company based out of Barcelona, Tropicfeel has created not one, but two of the most funded shoes on Kickstarter, setting their record in 2018, and then nearly matching it in 2019. With innovation practically woven into the company&#8217;s DNA, Tropicfeel developed the Jungle footwear as the latest evolution to their all-terrain footwear collection.</p>\n<p>Outwardly, the Jungle sneakers embody simplicity, with a design that&#8217;s an urban classic of sorts. The shoes come in four color options with a quick-drying fabric body that fits as comfortably as a sock would. The fabric features an upside-down 3D mesh, designed in collaboration with Ariaprene. The fabric is optimized for abrasion-resistance and long-lasting build quality, while using 7 recycled plastic bottles in its construction (in an effort to eliminate ocean waste). The fabric body is then capped off with special Sprint Laces on top that allow you to easily secure your shoes firmly around your feet, and a revolutionary outsole at its base, giving you the slip-resistance you need, whether you&#8217;re on the tarmac, on tiles, or on terrain.</p>\n<p>The innovation comes naturally to Tropicfeel, but so does focus on sustainability. Each pair of shoes recycles 14 bottles worth of ocean plastic, while even the soles contain 30% recycled EVA foam. By entirely skipping the traditional retail route and focusing on crowdfunding, Tropicfeel can design shoes to order, eliminating the need to store them in shops, pay hefty retail taxes, or warehouse costs across the globe. Moreover, the shoes are durable and built-to-last too. With a classic design and the ability to be worn everywhere (and a lightweight construction that makes them easy to pack), the Tropicfeel Jungle is all set to be the next pair of shoes you&#8217;ll never want to take off!</p>\n<p>Designer: Tropicfeel</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.tropicfeel.com/pages/jungle-cf?utm_source=newsletter&#38;utm_medium=Link&#38;utm_campaign=YankoDesigns\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><strong>Click Here to Buy Now: $95</strong></a> <del datetime=\"2021-04-01T12:07:49+00:00\">$119</del> (20% off). lifetime!","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=307084","description":"<div class=\"arve\" data-mode=\"normal\" data-provider=\"kickstarter\" data-src-no-ap=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime/widget/video.html\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"590.625\" src=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime/widget/video.html\" width=\"1050\"></iframe></p>\n<p></span></p>\n<p></span></p>\n</div>\n<p>Here&#8217;s a pencil designed to last a lifetime as well as write for a lifetime. The Wingback Mechanical Pencil is an expertly crafted all-metal writing/drawing instrument designed to work seamlessly for decades. Made from high-quality metals with well-engineered tolerances, the Wingback Mechanical Pencil looks premium and feels robust. Like any good piece of stationery, it&#8217;s weighted to give you a comfortable writing and drawing experience, measures a compact 117.5mm to fit perfectly in the crook of your hand, and it&#8217;s built to last&#8230; but its most remarkable feature actually sits under its hood, away from your eyes.</p>\n<p>Unlike most mechanical pencils, the Wingback focuses on the less tangible aspects of performance too. Sure, a pencil should be able to let you draw flowing lines, and let you ideate with relative ease&#8230; but what happens when you suddenly run out of lead in the middle of a sketch? Your thought-flow breaks and you spend a good 2 minutes opening the pencil, emptying the old lead piece out, and adding a new lead piece in. The Wingback Mechanical Pencil circumvents that problem with a cleverly designed interior. The pencil&#8217;s hollow body holds as many as 40 lead refills at a time, and a cleverly designed bespoke mechanism allows new leads to deploy as soon as the old lead finishes, allowing you to continuously write or draw without any break in your flow. In fact, designer Alasdair MacLaine claims that the pencil fits 10x more lead than traditional mechanical pencils, and can continuously write for 50 full kilometers, so you should only have to refill the lead tank a handful of times in a lifetime (that&#8217;s if you&#8217;re a serious sketch-bug!)</p>\n<p>The Wingback Mechanical Pencil is reminiscent of the London-based design studio&#8217;s Mechanical Pen design from 2019. It comes immaculately machined from metal, with three metallic options to choose from &#8211; Brass, Stainless Steel, and Black Steel (featuring a scratch-resistant tungsten carbide surface finish). The gripping area measures a comfortable 10mm in diameter and features a knurled texture that&#8217;s great to look at and even greater to hold.</p>\n<p>Pressing the top of the pencil triggers the unique all-metal propelling mechanism inside, which has been designed by Wingback in England and built specifically for this model by a specialist manufacturer in Japan. This mechanism lets you fit a stunning 2.4 meters worth of lead refills inside, while the clicking action deploys a new refill as soon as the old one finishes. A retractable lead sleeve, activated by holding down the clicker, allows the lead to be pushed back inside the Pencil, and prevents any unwanted lead-wobble as you write, giving you an entirely well-calibrated writing experience from start to end.</p>\n<p>Speaking of &#8216;from start to end&#8217;, that seems to be Wingback&#8217;s underlying philosophy too. Just like its 2019 Mechanical Pen, the Wingback Mechanical Pencil is built to outlast any other stationery you have. Its immaculately designed, engineered, and constructed body is made to last a lifetime (the brass variant should even develop a brilliant patina over the years), and with space for 40 lead refills, the pencil&#8217;s writing capacity will probably outlast your creativity too!</p>\n<p>The brand&#8217;s logo is discreetly engraved along the barrel using a pulsed fiber laser, and each Pencil comes with the option to add up to 50 characters on the reverse, making it an extra personal keepsake. With a subtle nod to its heritage and local construction, MADE IN ENGLAND is also unobtrusively engraved on the Pencil&#8217;s internal compartment. Wingback have also announced that the Mechanical Pencil will be offered with limited edition artist collaborations throughout April, so keep your eye on their campaign for each new release!</p>\n<p>Designer: Alasdair MacLaine of Wingback</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><strong>Click Here to Buy Now: $93</strong></a> <del datetime=\"2021-03-31T07:08:28+00:00\">$130</del> (33% off). Hurry, less than 12 hours left! Raised over $80,000.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308562\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/Wingback_all_metal_mechanical_pencil.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">The Designer&#8217;s All-metal Mechanical Pencil</h4>\n<p>Made in England by design studio Wingback, the Mechanical Pencil has a bespoke all-metal propelling mechanism that can fit up to 2.4m of lead – enough to keep you writing for over 50km.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308564\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-glorious-all-metal-mechanical-pencil-stores-enough-lead-to-last-you-an-entire-lifetime/Wingback_all_metal_mechanical_pencil_01.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"800\" /></a></p>\n<p>With a wide 10mm (3/8 inch) diameter and diamond knurled grip, it sits comfortably in the hand to reduce writing fatigue, while the satisfying weight of its materials encourages more time to be taken with every stroke.</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Mechanism</h4>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-309050\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-glorious-all-metal-mechanical-pencil-stores-enough-lead-to-last-you-an-entire-lifetime/Wingback_all_metal_mechanical_pencil_02.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"800\" /></a></p>\n<p>Their all-metal mechanism holds up to 2.4m of lead. Which should keep you writing, sketching, drawing and doodling for months or even years.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-309051\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-glorious-all-metal-mechanical-pencil-stores-enough-lead-to-last-you-an-entire-lifetime/Wingback_all_metal_mechanical_pencil_03.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"800\" /></a></p>\n<p>Customized designed from start to finish, the pencil&#8217;s mechanism is made in Iwaki, by Japan&#8217;s oldest mechanical pencil manufacturer (founded in 1909) with a track record for producing quality parts for the world&#8217;s most respected pencil brands.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308368\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-glorious-all-metal-mechanical-pencil-stores-enough-lead-to-last-you-an-entire-lifetime/Wingback_machined_mechanical_pen_08.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Personalization</h4>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308378\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-glorious-all-metal-mechanical-pencil-stores-enough-lead-to-last-you-an-entire-lifetime/Wingback_machined_mechanical_pen_13.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<p>Every Pencil is engraved with a pulsed fibre laser and can be personalized with up to 50 characters along the barrel – enough space for initials, a name or quote to make the pencil extra special for its owner.</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Wingback X Artist Series</h4>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-309052\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-glorious-all-metal-mechanical-pencil-stores-enough-lead-to-last-you-an-entire-lifetime/Wingback_all_metal_mechanical_pencil_04.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"800\" /></a></p>\n<p>Wingback have teamed up with select artists, illustrators and even cartographers from around the world. These special edition collaborations will be available in brass and stainless steel.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img src=\"https://ksr-ugc.imgix.net/assets/032/944/816/667ba26fa8149f9ced36248360bcfcdc_original.gif?ixlib=rb-2.1.0&#38;w=680&#38;fit=max&#38;v=1617189248&#38;auto=format&#38;gif-q=50&#38;q=92&#38;s=929c442ceedeb25e442ff5fa02d7c6a3\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"591\" /></a></p>\n<p><strong>Limited Edition Drop #1: Wingback X Anoushka Irukandji</strong> &#8211; This Brisbane-based artist&#8217;s henna-inspired “Terra Australis” design is a declaration of love for her adopted home country. “It&#8217;s inspired by the spectacular flora, everblooming trees and the beautiful shapes and textures in the leaves, bark and seed pods that I’m privileged to walk among every day,” she explains.</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Design &#38; Functionality</h4>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-309053\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-glorious-all-metal-mechanical-pencil-stores-enough-lead-to-last-you-an-entire-lifetime/Wingback_all_metal_mechanical_pencil_05.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"800\" /></a></p>\n<p>Over a year of design work and 20+ iterations has refined this design. A larger diameter barrel means your hand won&#8217;t fatigue as quickly as gripping a narrower pencil and the knurled barrel provides good purchase for your fingers.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-309054\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-glorious-all-metal-mechanical-pencil-stores-enough-lead-to-last-you-an-entire-lifetime/Wingback_all_metal_mechanical_pencil_06.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"800\" /></a></p>\n<p>The satisfying weight of the pencil also puts a little extra momentum behind straight lines and circles and also acts as a gentle reminder to take more time over your writing and drawing, achieving a neater result.</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Materials</h4>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img src=\"https://ksr-ugc.imgix.net/assets/032/933/415/d793c15ff4292e3055e09ec2ea7eae26_original.gif?ixlib=rb-2.1.0&#38;w=680&#38;fit=max&#38;v=1617119618&#38;auto=format&#38;gif-q=50&#38;q=92&#38;s=8b45bd1f27b74ac7a8ceceea873f6e00\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"591\" /></a></p>\n<p>All of the metal used to machine the pencil housing is sourced from European companies who supply the aerospace industry. Available in Brass, Stainless Steel and Black Steel (Tungsten Carbide).</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img src=\"https://ksr-ugc.imgix.net/assets/032/933/362/79e97e5365692ae743beab0c146a9e40_original.gif?ixlib=rb-2.1.0&#38;w=680&#38;fit=max&#38;v=1617119430&#38;auto=format&#38;gif-q=50&#38;q=92&#38;s=23269fabbb5622eb325f2554d1ca5265\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"591\" /></a></p>\n<p><strong>Brass: 40g / 1.41 oz &#8211; </strong>The heavier of the two, the brass pencil will develop a unique patina as its surface oxidizes and interacts with the natural oils in your hands. This pen will quickly look like a timeless tool, but can easily be polished up to its original luster.</p>\n<p><strong>Stainless Steel 304: 36g / 1.27oz &#8211; </strong>Slightly lighter than brass, stainless steel has a harder surface and will not oxidize over time. This means it will maintain its crisp aesthetic indefinitely.</p>\n<p><strong>Black Steel 304: 36g / 1.27oz &#8211; </strong>Black Steel rivals the exotic look of Damascus steel or titanium, with a sub-metallic lustre that reveals a glimmer of the steel beneath the surface. The Black Steel finish also serves a vital purpose in protecting the Wingback Pencil for the long haul.</p>\n<p>All parts are interchangeable, allowing you to mix and match brass, stainless steel and black steel parts if you back the full set.</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Engineering</h4>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-309055\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-glorious-all-metal-mechanical-pencil-stores-enough-lead-to-last-you-an-entire-lifetime/Wingback_all_metal_mechanical_pencil_07.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<p>The pencil&#8217;s machined casing is custom made from start to finish and they are proud to make this product in England using trusted local suppliers. A solid block of stainless steel or brass is CNC machined to produce incredibly precise parts which are a pleasure to use. Each one is individually inspected and tested to ensure it will withstand the test of time. Our manufacturing partner make predominantly aerospace components and have BS EN AS 9100 accreditation.</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Specification</h4>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-309056\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-glorious-all-metal-mechanical-pencil-stores-enough-lead-to-last-you-an-entire-lifetime/Wingback_all_metal_mechanical_pencil_08.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<p>The pencil is designed to be as compact as possible to fit discreetly into a bag or pocket for use on the go, but long enough to sit comfortably in the crook of your hand while drawing for long periods. The wide diameter makes it comfortable to use for long periods and strong enough to last a lifetime.</p>\n<p>&#8211; Diameter: Ø10mm / 3/8 Inch<br />\n&#8211; Height: 117.5mm / 4.63 Inch</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">The Finish</h4>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-309057\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-glorious-all-metal-mechanical-pencil-stores-enough-lead-to-last-you-an-entire-lifetime/Wingback_all_metal_mechanical_pencil_09.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"800\" /></a></p>\n<p>Machined finish to a surface roughness of 1.6 Ra (μm) with a 0.5mm perpendicular diamond knurl around the circumference. The surface roughness is visually smooth, but has a lovely tactility, the deliberate microscopic surface variation means that scratches picked up will be less prominent than on a smoother surface. The small knurling detail offers a good solid grip for long sessions.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-309058\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-glorious-all-metal-mechanical-pencil-stores-enough-lead-to-last-you-an-entire-lifetime/Wingback_all_metal_mechanical_pencil_10.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/maclainedesign/a-custom-mechanical-pencil-that-is-built-to-last-a-lifetime?ref=f4amni\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><strong>Click Here to Buy Now: $92</strong></a> <del datetime=\"2021-03-31T07:08:28+00:00\">$130</del> (30% off). 14:45:36","updatedTime":"2021-04-05 14:45:36","title":"Water-cooled terracotta tiles provide natural cooling to subway stations during the summer","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=303103","description":"<p><a href=\"https://discoverlexus.com/experiences/lexus-design-award-2021?utm_source=yankodesign&#38;utm_medium=article0207&#38;utm_campaign=yankodesign_lda2021\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-309099\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/water-cooled-terracotta-tiles-provide-natural-cooling-to-subway-stations-during-the-summer/Terracotta_Valley_Wind_2021_Lexus_Design_Award_finalist.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<p>A clever system of terracotta tiles with water channels woven between them is proving to be a natural, cost-effective way to reduce energy consumption for cooling down subway stations during the summer. Designed by Intsui Design, the Terracotta Valley Wind hopes to drastically reduce energy consumption in the summer by relying on terracotta&#8217;s naturally occurring evaporative cooling ability. The material is inherently inexpensive and easy to source, while Intsui Design&#8217;s clever tiling design is both eye-catching and functional, earning it a deserved Finalist spot at the LEXUS DESIGN AWARD 2021.</p>\n<p>The way the Terracotta Valley Wind cools spaces is simple and frankly ingenious. Water is fed through channels running through the inside of the tiles. The porous tiles absorb the water, which then evaporates through the outer surface, cooling the tile and the air around it. To circulate this cooled air, the Terracotta Valley Wind ingeniously uses the subway train&#8217;s movement as free energy! The trains whoosh through the station, pushing the cold air around as they go, acting exactly as a bellow pump would. The periodic nature of the train&#8217;s movement completely nullifies the Terracotta Valley Wind&#8217;s electrical needs, making it a cost-effective solution that requires absolutely no energy and emits zero pollution&#8230; while using reclaimed water all along, yet another abundant resource!</p>\n<p>The Terracotta Valley Wind&#8217;s brilliant use of evaporative cooling, reclaimed water, and the moving train&#8217;s wind energy to uniformly cool subway stations makes it the perfect candidate for the LEXUS DESIGN AWARD 2021, aligning wonderfully with its theme of &#8220;Design for a Better Tomorrow&#8221;. Currently in its 9th year, the Lexus Design Award is on a mission to ideate and innovate for a better future for humanity as well as for the planet. With its underlying theme of “Design for a Better Tomorrow”, the awards program looks at solutions that have a uniquely positive impact on society, humanity, and in the process, to reward a new generation of designers for their impactful ideas. Creating the perfect environment for a design to grow, LEXUS helps engineer ideas into real, innovative solutions. Apart from accelerating, developing, and promoting design projects, the Lexus Design Award helps kickstart design careers too, with exclusive mentorships from international design stalwarts like Joe Doucet, Mariam Kamara, Sabine Marcelis and Sputniko!, as well as funding for prototypes (up to 3 million Japanese Yen or $25,000 per project) and the opportunity to have your work judged by the biggest figures in design in the final Grand Prix competition. This year’s judges include Paola Antonelli (Senior Curator at MoMA), Dong Gong (Founder and Principal Designer at Vector Architects), Greg Lynn (Architect and CEO at Piaggio Fast Forward), and Simon Humphries (Head of Toyota and Lexus Global Design).</p>\n<p>The Terracotta Valley Wind is one of the six finalists of the LEXUS DESIGN AWARD 2021. Stay tuned as <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/tag/lexus-design-award-2021/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">we feature all the finalist designs</a> following the Grand Prix Winner Announcement here on Yanko Design!</p>\n<p>Designer: Intsui Design</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://discoverlexus.com/experiences/lexus-design-award-2021?utm_source=yankodesign&#38;utm_medium=article0207&#38;utm_campaign=yankodesign_lda2021\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><strong>Click Here to See All Six Lexus Design Awards Finalists!</strong></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://discoverlexus.com/experiences/lexus-design-award-2021?utm_source=yankodesign&#38;utm_medium=article0207&#38;utm_campaign=yankodesign_lda2021\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308695\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/water-cooled-terracotta-tiles-provide-natural-cooling-to-subway-stations-during-the-summer/Lexus_Design_Award_2021_Terracotta_Valley_Wind_01.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Terracotta Valley Wind</h4>\n<p>A terracotta evaporative cooling system that cools subway stations during summer and reduces energy consumption. Terracotta is an inexpensive and accessible clay material. Its nature allows water to quickly evaporate, while utilizing the unused wind resource in subway stations, maximizing the value of train-induced wind.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://discoverlexus.com/experiences/lexus-design-award-2021?utm_source=yankodesign&#38;utm_medium=article0207&#38;utm_campaign=yankodesign_lda2021\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308697\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/water-cooled-terracotta-tiles-provide-natural-cooling-to-subway-stations-during-the-summer/Lexus_Design_Award_2021_Terracotta_Valley_Wind_03.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<p>The team studied that in a ventilated environment, terracotta’s porous nature allows for water to easily move through the walls, which accelerates the evaporation speed of the water. By transmuting water to air, it absorbs a relatively large amount of heat, effectively reducing the temperature of the environment.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://discoverlexus.com/experiences/lexus-design-award-2021?utm_source=yankodesign&#38;utm_medium=article0207&#38;utm_campaign=yankodesign_lda2021\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308696\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/water-cooled-terracotta-tiles-provide-natural-cooling-to-subway-stations-during-the-summer/Lexus_Design_Award_2021_Terracotta_Valley_Wind_02.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<p>This principle of terracotta can work perfectly with the train-induced wind and airflow in the subway station. The concept of Terracotta Valley Wind as in-station passive cooling wall is composed of spliced terracotta slabs, with an automatic water supply system consist of stainless steelframe implanted with water pipes. Ideally, the slabs are humidified by reclaimed water, which evaporates faster when the wind is induced by train, and thus to achieve a cooling effect in the subway station. The whole system is pollution-free and does not require any electricity.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://discoverlexus.com/experiences/lexus-design-award-2021?utm_source=yankodesign&#38;utm_medium=article0207&#38;utm_campaign=yankodesign_lda2021\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-300573\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/02/this-innovative-skylight-uses-light-from-the-sun-to-purify-drinking-water/lexus_design_awards_2021_02.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"807\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://discoverlexus.com/experiences/lexus-design-award-2021?utm_source=yankodesign&#38;utm_medium=article0207&#38;utm_campaign=yankodesign_lda2021\" Jetsons!","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=308538","description":"<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308544\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/308538/01_zhikamaster_orionstar_coffeerobot.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>If you sometimes feel like a <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/tag/robot/\">robot</a> before your first cup of <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/tag/coffee/\">coffee</a>, you’re in good company. Without even fully opening my eyes, I get my first cup of coffee going for the morning, and while it brews I get myself ready. On good days, I turn my stove off on time, and on other days, I gulp down a burnt cup of coffee. Coffee is a necessary part of the day for a lot of us and having that perfect cup in the morning might be all we need to get our day off on the right foot. To save us from those &#8216;other days,&#8217; Beijing’s Orion Star Technology Co. Ltd. recently designed a robotic coffeemaking system, the Zhi Ka Master that was shortlisted at 2021’s iF Design Awards.</p>\n<p>Zhi Ka Master is a coffee-making system that employs the use of twin-arm robotics to perform traditional coffee and tea brewing for hand-poured, automated cups of coffee. The entire system comprises a twin-arm, six-axis robot and accompanying work table. Twin-arm robotic systems are typically chosen for their efficient and automated execution of more involved assembly operations. Through bi-manual manipulation, twin-arm robots can perform complicated tasks in a human-like manner. The incorporation of twin-arm robotics for Zhi Ka Master and a bionic profile design equips the robot with enough know-how to stimulate masterful coffee or tea-making methods with the push of a button. A pre-sized and programmed worktable is used to keep all the machines and tools necessary to make any drink on a typical coffee menu.</p>\n<p>You’re like me if your coffee order comes with some conditions: <em>an extra shot of espresso please and not too much ice</em>. Rest assured, Zhi Ka Master knows how to receive special input for specific coffee orders that veer from the menu. Through integrated software, Zhi Ka Master can make coffee and tea drinks for specific tastes all without human intervention. So maybe, don’t push that button.</p>\n<p>Designer: <a href=\"https://www.orionstar.com/index\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Orion Star Technology Co. Ltd.</a></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308543\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/308538/02_zhikamaster_orionstar_coffeerobot.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>Zhi Ka Master is a six-axis, twin-arm robot coffeemaker.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308542\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/308538/03_zhikamaster_orionstar_coffeerobot.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>Integrated software adjusts the robot&#8217;s mechanical grip to fit whatever item it grasps.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308541\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/308538/04_zhikamaster_orionstar_coffeerobot.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>Through a built-in RGB camera, the robot performs duties and responds to feedback in real-time to ensure safe operation.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308540\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/308538/05_zhikamaster_orionstar_coffeerobot.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>Equipped with an emergency stop button, Zhi Ka Master prioritizes safety even before coffee.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308539\" 14:45:36","updatedTime":"2021-04-05 14:45:36","title":"These students designed a way of repurposing chewing gum to make skateboard wheels!","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=308945","description":"<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308947\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/308945/05_gumwheels_hugomaupetitvivianfischer_chewinggumskateboardwheels.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>The plastics used to build car tires are the same plastics used to make chewing gum. From the moment we spit our gum onto the ground, it will take upwards of 50 years for that one piece to even begin decomposition. Noticing the wasted potential of chewing gum and the harmful effects it poses on the <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/tag/sustainable-design/\">environment</a>, design students Hugo Maupetit and Vivian Fischer decided to collect wads of discarded chewing gum out of which they molded and constructed <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/tag/rubber/\">wheels</a> for skateboards.</p>\n<p>After noticing that discarded chewing gum, made from synthetic rubbers, could be repurposed to construct wheels for skateboards, Maupetit and Fischer visualized a future partnership with Mentos and Vans. In the imagined collaboration, they worked together to take the gum from the streets and bring the gum back to the streets in a sustainable way. “Our initiative is supposed to clean the streets in a sustainable way. That is why we invented a system that will transform used wheels and turn them into new ones,” Maupetit and Fischer explained. “No more waste is created and the material stays in use.”</p>\n<p>Initiating the collaboration, Maupetit and Fischer suggested that ‘gum boards’ be installed throughout their university city of Nantes, where residents could tack their finished chewing gum. As the gum boards filled up, the individual pieces would be collected, cleaned, molded together with a stabilizing agent, and stained with natural dye to form the wheels’ bases. The vibrant color of chewing gum along with its rubbery texture makes it a playful, yet tough choice for tire production.</p>\n<p>People have been chewing on gum since the 1860s, but it was only after World War II that manufacturers began using synthetic rubbers, like polyethylene and polyvinyl acetate to make chewing gum. Plastics, like synthetic rubber, are able to be molded, pressed, and hardened into different shapes, making the building material relatively durable and easy to work with. Plus, there’s no shortage of supply– it’s everywhere.</p>\n<p>Designers: Hugo Maupetit and Vivian Fischer</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308950\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/308945/02_gumwheels_hugomaupetitvivianfischer_chewinggumskateboardwheels.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>In an imagined collaboration with Vans and Mentos, Maupetit and Fischer conceived a mode of operations for their &#8220;Off The Street&#8221; gum-wheel initiative, including gum collection and tire production.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308948\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/308945/04_gumwheels_hugomaupetitvivianfischer_chewinggumskateboardwheels.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>Gum boards throughout the city designate a spot for passersby to tack their gum for future collection.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308949\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/308945/03_gumwheels_hugomaupetitvivianfischer_chewinggumskateboardwheels.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>Once the gum boards are filled up, they&#8217;ll be collected for future cleaning, molding, and staining.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308951\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/04/308945/01_gumwheels_hugomaupetitvivianfischer_chewinggumskateboardwheels.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>Finally, following the mold and stain manufacturing process, wheels can be made available in stores for skateboarders to purchase.</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?a=sUWfKu5u504:1KlOQDJaroY:yIl2AUoC8zA\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?d=yIl2AUoC8zA\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a 14:45:36","updatedTime":"2021-04-05 14:45:36","title":"3D printed product designs that exhibit the endless possibilities of this innovative technique!","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=308855","description":"<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/08/coral-reef/12-terracotta_reef_yankodesign-1.jpg\" /></p>\n<p>Designers and architects all over the world are now adopting 3D Printing for the creation of almost all types of products and structures! It&#8217;s a technique that has gained a lot of momentum, owing to its simple and innovative nature. But designers aren&#8217;t employing 3D printing only to create basic models, they&#8217;re utilizing this technique in mind-blowing ways as well! From 3D printed artificial coral reefs to a menacing automotive design with 3D printed parts, the scope of this dependable technique is unlimited! In fact, did you know, lunar habitats for the moon are being 3D printed as well? There&#8217;s honestly nothing that cannot be 3D printed these days, the possibilities are endless, and we&#8217;re super excited to see what else is in store! For now, dive into this collection of humble yet groundbreaking 3D printed designs!</p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/08/coral-reef/0-terracotta_reef_yankodesign-1.jpg\" /></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/08/coral-reef/07-terracotta_reef_yankodesign-1.jpg\" /></p>\n<p>Hong Kong saw an 80% decline in the coral population in Double Island, Sai Kung, over the past decade and that drove the team to come up with a solution that would not only help that region but also the rest of the world that was blessed with corals. The team from Swire Institute of Marine Science (SWIMS) of the University of Hong Kong (HKU) and its Robotic Fabrication Lab of the faculty of architecture worked together to <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2020/08/05/these-3d-printed-terracotta-tiles-along-hong-kongs-coast-are-designed-to-revive-the-marine-coral-life/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">3D print terra-cotta tiles</a> that will act as artificial reefs. The result is a mesmerizing, organic swirl of line and negative space that reads like a burnt orange topographic map—and mimics the natural patterns of the coral itself. Why terra-cotta? It’s highly porous with “nice surface micro-texture” for marine organisms to latch on to, says team member Dave Baker, and an eco-friendly alternative to conventional materials such as cement or metal, the HKU team says.</p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/04/MH19_3D_printed_handle.jpg\" /></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/04/MH19_3D_printed_handle_01.jpg\" /></p>\n<p class=\"post-without-image\">The shape of the handy tool called <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2020/04/18/the-3d-printed-mh-19-multifunctional-tool-reduces-contact-risk-when-you-step-out-for-essential-items/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">MH-19</a> is inspired by <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/tag/face-mask/\">protection masks</a> and has solved yet another problem using design. Gloves are single-use items that generate more waste if used by everyone to do everyday things. Gloves can be left aside for the healthcare professionals who need them the most while we can use reusable handles like this for our daily essential outdoor tasks. Innovation has the power to be simple yet mighty effective in its purpose. 3D printers are currently a valuable tool in this fight and the global design community is doing everything they can to support the healthcare professionals, engineers as well as the general public through their creativity.</p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/05/this-futuristic-custom-e-bike-comes-with-an-organic/fuller_moto_majestic_1.jpg\" /></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/05/this-futuristic-custom-e-bike-comes-with-an-organic/fuller_moto_majestic_2.jpg\" /></p>\n<p class=\"post-without-image\">The <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2020/05/07/this-futuristic-custom-e-bike-comes-with-organic-3d-printed-details-and-transparent-wheel-rims/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">2029 e-bike</a> brings art-deco and automotive design into the future, with its unusual combination of clean-cut geometric shapes brought about by sheet-metal fabrication, along with bone-inspired generative-design details 3D printed in metal. The bike is an amalgamation of styles that pays a hat-tip to the revolutionary design of the 1929 Majestic, built by George Roy. Ninety years later, Bryan Fuller and his team at Fuller Moto decided to push boundaries with bike design. Created as a commissioned piece for the Haas Moto Museum and Sculpture Gallery, the bike incorporates design trends and technologies that are indicative of the future of automotive design. The stunning 2029 comes with an electric drivetrain, fully enclosed aluminum body, hub-centric steering, transparent PolyCarbonate wheels, and 3D printed bike parts, furnished out of Titanium.</p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/08/can-niveas-3d-printed-shower-gel-refill-station-prototype-really-reduce-plastic-packaging-waste/01-nivea_yankodesign.jpg\" /></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/08/can-niveas-3d-printed-shower-gel-refill-station-prototype-really-reduce-plastic-packaging-waste/09-nivea_yankodesign.jpg\" /></p>\n<p class=\"post-without-image\">NIVEA’s parent company is German giant Beiersdorf and they are on a mission to reduce packaging waste by minimizing and closing their material cycles. And for NIVEA that meant launching a shower gel refill station! Now it is a good first step and has its pros but also has some cons. The biggest con is that shower gels themselves are not good for the environment and there is no way to know how many bottles actually get rinsed clean before they are recycled – otherwise, it doesn’t work. Shower gels also need a lot of water to be made, and as climate change makes the world hotter/drier, the water crisis is already a big issue in many countries. A solution to that? Bar soaps! NIVEA makes those too, they use less water and can be packaged in the recycled paper – that is the real solution but if this <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2020/08/13/can-niveas-3d-printed-shower-gel-refill-station-prototype-really-reduce-plastic-packaging-waste/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">refill station</a> reduces some plastic waste and sparks a movement for the brand to take bigger steps, then we are here to see it. The prototype is going to be tested in select locations where the brand will gather data on how consumers are interacting, feeling, reacting to the concept of reusable bottles. The prototype machine was made with their in-house 3D printers<em>. </em>NIVEA hopes that with this refill station they will make it convenient for consumers to reuse containers and reduce plastic usage.</p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/09/auto-draft/coral_lighting_collection_1.jpg\" /></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/09/auto-draft/coral_lighting_collection_2.jpg\" /></p>\n<p class=\"post-without-image\">Say hello to Timor, Sargasso, and Celebes, three members of <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2020/09/25/these-3d-printed-lamps-were-designed-using-algorithms-that-copy-coral-growth-patterns/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">John’s Coral Lighting Collection</a>. Inspired by different styles of corals, the lamps come with varying aesthetics that reflect the visual characteristics of each coral type. The way John went about creating these unique lights was to first develop the computational design algorithms that mimic growth patterns found in nature. “The lighting collection is my way of paying tribute to the beauty of the ocean. As a veteran surfer, I’ve experienced the power and beauty of the ocean while enjoying each wave as its own unique moment in time. One of many magical living structures in our great oceans is coral. With a diverse range of colors, shapes, and scales, coral is an entire ecosystem of thriving life. My lighting celebrates this life”, says Mauriello.</p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/05/this-3d-printed-structure-prevents-your-face-mask-from-collapsing-as-you-breathe/cannula_mask_1.jpg\" /></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/05/this-3d-printed-structure-prevents-your-face-mask-from-collapsing-as-you-breathe/cannula_mask_5.jpg\" /></p>\n<p class=\"post-without-image\">What we really need is for everyone to wear face-masks that prevent the transmission of germs. What we DON’T need is for those face-masks to make it harder for us to breathe, right? As you inhale, most flimsy fabric masks collapse inwards because of the negative air pressure created inside the mask… it’s honestly something most people can deal with, but if you’re someone with pre-existing respiratory difficulties, it could make regular breathing rather difficult. <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2020/05/13/this-3d-printed-structure-prevents-your-face-mask-from-collapsing-as-you-breathe/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">The Cannula mask</a> avoids this problem with its reinforcing endoskeleton. A thin plastic grille, this skeleton gives the mask its defining structure, preventing it from pressing against your face the same way a hanger prevents clothes from getting crushed by retaining its shape. Designed to be worn by people with respiratory difficulties, the endoskeleton even comes with a hollow spine that allows you to plug a nasal cannula into it, letting you direct fresh oxygen right to the wearer’s nose; effectively allowing them to inhale and exhale freely without worrying about a flimsy mask smothering them every time they try to breathe.</p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2019/04/auto-draft/sandvik_unbreakable_guitar_1.jpg\" /></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2019/04/auto-draft/sandvik_unbreakable_guitar_2.jpg\" /></p>\n<p class=\"post-without-image\">A lot of moments in rock history are defined by the iconic guitar-smash… and while I personally don’t think it’s particularly nice to smash musical equipment, what if you designed a guitar that, if you look at the image immediately below, couldn’t be smashed? That’s what Sandvik decided to do. Designed to show off their advanced titanium additive printing techniques (and also their engineering prowess), they designed the <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2019/04/16/this-3d-printed-metal-guitar-is-absolutely-indestructible/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">world’s first guitar that can’t be smashed</a>. Literally. Many have even tried, including rockstar Yngwie Malmsteen, who managed to wreck his stage amps and monitors but couldn’t get the guitar to even as much as deform. Sandvik partnered with guitar-designer Andy Holt over what sounds like a pretty unusual design brief… Designing an electric guitar that was virtually indestructible, but also sounded incredibly good. The design process included hours of analyzing footage of guitars being smashed (many by Malmsteen himself) to analyze the biggest points of weaknesses.</p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/08/Lytte_HarmoniQ_worlds_first_3D_acoustic_earbuds_hero.jpg\" /></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/08/these-3d-printed-tws-earbuds-were-designed-to-provide-incredible-sound-and-a-perfect-fit/Lytte_HarmoniQ_worlds_first_3D_acoustic_earbuds_01.jpg\" /></p>\n<p class=\"post-without-image\"><a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2020/08/06/these-3d-printed-tws-earbuds-were-designed-to-provide-incredible-sound-and-a-perfect-fit/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">The TWS earphones’</a> unique shape comes with a specially designed 3D acoustic chamber that helps make the audio sound richer, with better, more distinct basslines… while also helping reduce sound distortion as well as providing organic noise isolation of up to -35 db, allowing it to rival the Airpods Pro’s active noise cancellation tech just through its ergonomic design. The amount of careful consideration built into the Lytte HarmoniQ is truly remarkable. Each earphone casing is meticulously 3D printed using DLP printing tech (a feature that allows it to have that unique acoustic chamber shape) and hand-polished to look as remarkable as it does. Just like most smart earphones, the Lytte HarmoniQ supports iOS as well as Android integration, with the ability to tap, double-tap, and long-press to control music playback as well as smartphone functions (including summoning the phone’s voice AI).</p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-credit-card-sized-antenna-turns-5g-signals-into-wireless-power-for-iot-devices/3D-printed-5G-wave-harnessing-antenna-by-Georgia-Institute-of-Technology-ATHENA-lab_1.jpg\" /></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-credit-card-sized-antenna-turns-5g-signals-into-wireless-power-for-iot-devices/3D-printed-5G-wave-harnessing-antenna-by-Georgia-Institute-of-Technology-ATHENA-lab-4.jpg\" /></p>\n<p class=\"post-without-image\"><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">Harvesting abundant sources of </span><a class=\"editor-rtfLink\" href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/tag/renewable-energy/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">renewable energy</span></a><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> and then converting them into something valuable has been the quest humankind has been on for decades. This makes even more sense in current times when we are on the brink of exhausting earth’s vital resources, causing unrepairable harm to the planet. As scouts of this very quest, the team at Georgia Tech’s ATHENA lab has created a </span><a class=\"editor-rtfLink\" href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/tag/3d-printed/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">3D-printed</span></a><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> energy harvesting antenna that’s capable of garnering electromagnetic energy of the 5G signals to juice modern-day gadgets. The technology is literally about putting the overcapacity 5G network bandwidth to judicious use – turning it into a wireless power grid that could shape the future of our relentless energy requirements for </span><a class=\"editor-rtfLink\" href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/tag/iot\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">IoT devices</span></a><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> or mobile devices. </span><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">They’ve created <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2021/03/30/this-credit-card-sized-antenna-harvests-energy-from-5g-signals-into-wireless-power-for-iot-devices/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">a flexible Rotman lens-based rectifying antenna</a> (rectenna) that can collect the millimeter-wave in the 28-GHz band – the first of its kind. Previously there have been attempts to harvest the 24 or 35 GHz frequencies, but they were not practical since they only worked when they are in sight of the 5G base station.</span></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2018/12/the-worlds-first-3d-printed-conference-table/rexaxon_3d_printed_conference_table_layout.jpg\" alt=\"rexaxon_3d_printed_conference_table_layout\" /></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2018/12/rex/rex_03.jpg\" alt=\"rex_03\" /></p>\n<p>Does your company’s conference room need a little inspiration? This <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2018/12/12/the-worlds-first-3d-printed-conference-table/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">far-out office furniture</a> is designed to liven up your workspace. It’s entirely 3D-printed which results in smooth transitions and curves throughout. With its three-dimensional Voronoi pattern, it sports an organic, liquid-like shape that’s sure to be a conversation starter and something to get your team’s wheels turning.</p>\n<div eless-power-for-iot-devices/3D-printed-5G-wave-harnessing-antenna-by-Georgia-Institute-of-Technology-ATHENA-lab_1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn59@2020_2/2021/04/05/06-46-03-770_ba91ec0574e85333.webp","https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2021/03/this-credit-card-sized-antenna-turns-5g-signals-into-wireless-power-for-iot-devices/3D-printed-5G-wave-harnessing-antenna-by-Georgia-Institute-of-Technology-ATHENA-lab-4.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn82@2020_1/2021/04/05/06-46-03-013_d6617415f3b59955.webp","https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2018/12/the-worlds-first-3d-printed-conference-table/rexaxon_3d_printed_conference_table_layout.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn3@2020_2/2021/04/05/06-46-05-819_a4e694238448d764.webp","https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2018/12/rex/rex_03.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn85@2020_4/2021/04/05/06-46-02-944_01921e68b0ac5950.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn67@2020_3/2021/04/05/06-46-04-338_be70ddf18521ce99.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?i=PscidQXXbR8:LRSxZPbPFrE:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn93@2020_4/2021/04/05/06-46-02-725_ca3c81cfbb3ff189.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?d=7Q72WNTAKBA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn79@2020_4/2021/04/05/06-46-02-784_a7bab000502b2c11.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?i=PscidQXXbR8:LRSxZPbPFrE:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn4@2020_4/2021/04/05/06-46-03-576_7425181a1a5a0337.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?i=PscidQXXbR8:LRSxZPbPFrE:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn5@2020_2/2021/04/05/06-46-02-872_557bdd93171e60c0.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn43@2020_6/2021/04/05/06-46-03-847_19238f9c81aa1a56.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/yankodesign/~4/PscidQXXbR8":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn94@2020_5/2021/04/05/06-46-02-903_79e19977d26398e6.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1617605136665},{"createdTime":"2021-04-05 sandbox=\"allow-scripts allow-same-origin allow-presentation allow-popups allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox allow-forms\" scrolling=\"no\" src=\"https://player.vimeo.com/video/510338930?dnt=1&#038;app_id=122963&#038;html5=1&#038;title=1&#038;byline=0&#038;portrait=0&#038;autoplay=0\" width=\"1050\"></iframe></p>\n<p></span></p>\n<p></span></p>\n</div>\n<p>The digital world has such a firm grip on our lives, we can’t imagine even a single day without at least one thing that is somehow unrelated to the digital realms. Be it entertainment while at home or commuting in our vehicles. Especially in the case of <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/category/automotive/\">cars</a>, manufacturers are making a swift move towards a connected environment, and future-forward interiors that are laden with <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/category/technology/\">technology</a>. On the flip side, for people who crave minimalism and peace of mind, it can be a cliché – something that HS Pforzheim MA student Oscar Johansson wants to address with his Volvo Haven concept car penned in collaboration with the <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/tag/volvo/\">Volvo</a> Design team as a part of his thesis project.</p>\n<p>Oscar has taken a bold detour from the cult belief of stuffing modern-day cars with tech-savvy upgrades – virtually treading the opposing direction, taking us back to the ways of nature, and a private space where you can finally feel at peace after a grueling week. The futuristic AWD electric car is devoid of any fancy digital dashboard displays or screens to keep up with all the HUD details about the surroundings of the car. Volvo Haven has a UX tunnel enclosure right in the middle running the length of the car that houses plants, algae, and moss which grow naturally since there are opening at each end to let in the elements – rain, snow, pollen, frost, slush or dirt. The self-driving lounge car minus any steering input or the usual vehicular aids is all about relaxing as your travel for a much needed digital detox.</p>\n<p>Most of the car has transparent body paneling, including the transparent gull-winged doors for an ultra-airy feel. Volvo Haven adopts an aerodynamic design on the outside highlighted by the sweeping lines, lending the vehicle a very charming personality overall. Those elements look somewhat similar to the <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2021/03/14/this-edgy-volvo-lounge-car-redefines-autonomous-luxury-travel-of-the-future/\">Volvo concept car by Roman Zenin</a> which also adopts a very airy element with a focus on the lounging experience. The fat wheel configuration makes us presume it is a performance concept ready for any thrilling skirmish after the relaxing ride for the most part of the journey. Overall, an intuitive concept car design that embodies the aspect of bringing nature inside while driving.</p>\n<p>Designer: Oscar Johansson and Volvo Design</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-308884\"
